       8             :  *       COMPUTATION OF SPECIAL FUNCTIONS

      10             :  *          Shanjie Zhang and Jianming Jin
      11             :  *
      12             :  *       Copyrighted but permission granted to use code in programs.
      13             :  *       Buy their book:
      14             :  *
      15             :  *          Shanjie Zhang, Jianming Jin,
      16             :  *          Computation of Special Functions,
      17             :  *          Wiley, 1996,
      18             :  *          ISBN: 0-471-11963-6,
      19             :  *          LC: QA351.C45.
      20             :  * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * *
      21             :  *
      22             :  *       Scipy changes:
      23             :  *       - Compiled into a single source file and changed REAL To DBLE throughout.
      24             :  *       - Changed according to ERRATA.
      25             :  *       - Changed GAMMA to GAMMA2 and PSI to PSI_SPEC to avoid potential conflicts.
      26             :  *       - Made functions return sf_error codes in ISFER variables instead
      27             :  *         of printing warnings. The codes are
      28             :  *         - SF_ERROR_OK        = 0: no error
      29             :  *         - SF_ERROR_SINGULAR  = 1: singularity encountered
      30             :  *         - SF_ERROR_UNDERFLOW = 2: floating point underflow
      31             :  *         - SF_ERROR_OVERFLOW  = 3: floating point overflow
      32             :  *         - SF_ERROR_SLOW      = 4: too many iterations required
      33             :  *         - SF_ERROR_LOSS      = 5: loss of precision
      34             :  *         - SF_ERROR_NO_RESULT = 6: no result obtained
      35             :  *         - SF_ERROR_DOMAIN    = 7: out of domain
      36             :  *         - SF_ERROR_ARG       = 8: invalid input parameter
      37             :  *         - SF_ERROR_OTHER     = 9: unclassified error
      38             :  *       - Improved initial guesses for roots in JYZO.
      39             :  *
      40             :  *
      41             :  */
